<span id="freeTextContainer8406110459923407182">I am a huge fan of J. Lynn. She does NA and she does it well. I initially had to ponder this as I sometimes base a whole book on my issue with one character...I just could not do this here because she created young adult characters with angsty drama and gave them romantic tales with the perfect blend of heat and sweet. Exactly what I wanted.<br/><br/>So Cameron Hamilton started this series and held the bar so high. Well move over because Jackson James has arrived!<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411599607i/11253930._SY540_.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/>HEY BARTENDER! Just once I would love to </span>
  <span id="freeText8406110459923407182" style="display:none">I am a huge fan of J. Lynn. She does NA and she does it well. I initially had to ponder this as I sometimes base a whole book on my issue with one character...I just could not do this here because she created young adult characters with angsty drama and gave them romantic tales with the perfect blend of heat and sweet. Exactly what I wanted.<br><br>So Cameron Hamilton started this series and held the bar so high. Well move over because Jackson James has arrived!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411599607i/11253930._SY540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>HEY BARTENDER! Just once I would love to jump into a book and become fictional!<br><br>Calla...you lucky gal, while I cant say you were "it" for me...or him, but I understood you!<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411599652i/11253938._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>In case you forget, she is the quite, shy friend. The awkward roomie who was always on the outside looking in. She has a mysterious past...and has the physical scars to prove the harsh affects of it. She covers her scars and she blends into college life as easily as the lies she tells.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1411599607ra/11253931.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>When the ghosts of her past invade her present and halt her future she turns toward that past begrudgingly...she returns HOME. In the hunt to get her life back she is unprepared for the sexy, sweet talking Jax James to make her business his own! IF only she could let down her walls...<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411599607i/11253932.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>So what we have here is a bit of a tragic tale...Calla's life is basically in the hole! From financial hardships, familial loss, potential death threats, and a whole lotta WTF is going on in my life. We also have an amazing man who is sexy on the outside and truly beautiful on the inside. Jax and Calla have a fun, flirty attraction that develops sweetly and quite emotionally. OH THOSE KISSES...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1411599607ra/11253933.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411599607i/11253934._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I cannot say that Calla is the best heroine. I admit many will get irritated with her early and often...she is very naïve and she is a vortex of insecurity. I often lost my cool with her actions, but then Jax...oh Jax...melt the panties right off of ya! Dear lord...so sweet, so damn sexy...he made her feel safe, loved and beautiful with every word and touch! He alone is worth the time invested here!<br><br>So I enjoyed this...a lot! Cam and Avery still hold my heart for fave couple, but this story of Jax and Calla is probably my favorite! Perhaps the tone was a bit harsher, the conflict more dire, and the overall relationship more realistic than the previous tales. The NA tone was set well and the intimacy was done very well! </span>

<div id="review_620277758" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/620277758" />
    <a title="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie"><img alt="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1514769932p2/3275325.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/620277758?book_show_action=true">May 20, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " href="/user/show/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie">Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9780062294814" href="/book/show/18738866-stay-with-me">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie?shelf=read-in-2014">read-in-2014</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie?shelf=emotional-angsty-books">emotional-angsty-books</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer620277758" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9911472698127112468"><i>Stay With Me</i> is Calla's story. She goes to college with the rest of the gang from the prior books, that is, until she finds out her tuition check bounced and all her funds are gone. Determined to find out what happened, she takes off to the place she thought she'd never return.<br/><br/>Well, here I was thinking this was going to be another book like the rest but oh no, this book took a left turn down dark and dirty street. And get your mind out of the gutter, I'm not talking about sex (although that was </span>
  <span id="freeText9911472698127112468" style="display:none"><i>Stay With Me</i> is Calla's story. She goes to college with the rest of the gang from the prior books, that is, until she finds out her tuition check bounced and all her funds are gone. Determined to find out what happened, she takes off to the place she thought she'd never return.<br><br>Well, here I was thinking this was going to be another book like the rest but oh no, this book took a left turn down dark and dirty street. And get your mind out of the gutter, I'm not talking about sex (although that was quite yummy-licous), I'm talking drugs, violence and thugs. That's right, it was quite a wild ride. <br><br>Calla returns to her hometown to find her mom only it turns out, her mom's on the run from some very bad people. Since she's low on funds, she heads to her mom's bar to see if she can find anything out. To her surprised, the bar is in good shape, physically and financially, and it appears to be due to a very handsome bartender named Jax. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411696664i/11266314.jpg" width="300" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>We find out that Jax is an ex marine who came to town at the advice of one of his friends, Reece, who just happens to be a police officer. Jax doesn't hesitate to let Calla know he's into her and into her in a big way. And <i>that's</i> really sexy! <br><br>Poor Calla, because of a horrible event in her childhood, she's left with some physical scars that have done quite a job on her mentally as well. So she's never really had a boyfriend or been kissed and she's twenty-one. Jax makes no bones about it that he's all set to remedy that. Calla can't imagine why he would be the least bit interested so she pushes him away. It always made me laugh when she just blurted out thing. <br><br>Intent on making her own way as much as possible, she goes to stay at her mom's house which unfortunately used to be the neighborhood drug house. Here's where I had the majority of my problems, not only is the house <i>not</i> safe but it's dirtier than hell and SHE NEVER CLEANS IT!! I digress, she does wash the sheets at least. I realize she doesn't have much money but she does have people willing to help her and that she can stay with. It just really creeped me out!<br><br>Anyway, so not only does Calla have to deal with her mom being on the run but now that the thugs know she's in town, they want <i>her</i> to find her mom...and they're not too nice about it. Luckily, Jax is all too willing to help her out. And when she doesn't want to think about those things, he knows <i>exactly</i> what to do to get her mind off of it. ;)<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1403998026i/10177090.jpg" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I really liked Jax...for the most part, however, there is one teeny, tiny bit that I didn't understand <b>at. all.</b> and it ends with a double E. Come on...how could he not know it wasn't okay? That was a real let down. <br><br>I did love that Cam, Avery, Teresa and Jase were included in the story quite a bit. I loved when the girls all opened up to each other and I loved how the guys were so protective!<br><br>Two shout-outs go to Calla's "Uncle" Clyde - who seemed like a big ol' teddy bear and I loved that he called her "Baby Girl" (I wanna go to taco night!) - and to Katie - OMG, she is sooo hilarious...the things that came out of her mouth! Gotta love it even if it did start to lose its charm towards the end. (BTW, what was going on with Nick? I'd like more of his story.) <br><br>The story focuses A LOT on Calla's scars and while I know it's something terrible to deal with, in the beginning, it was just too much. It really began to turn me off until things started to get steamy and then it became quite sweet and helped to understand where Jax was coming from.<br><br>Yes, this book is quite steamy. Calla can definitely check quite a few things off her list. <br><br>Overall, I really like the story and this series is one I really enjoy. I do hate that there wasn't an epilogue. I really needed some more happy at the end. <br><br>As far as who's story is next, I don't have a clue. All the friends at college are now paired up but we did get to meet a few new possible pairings in Calla's hometown...so who knows? I do know it will be good and I will definitely be reading it. <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1387933324ra/7701256.gif" width="400" height="070" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>
  <u>Favorite quotes</u>
</b><br><br>♥ “Well, my fantasies involving nurses in little white skirts just got a whole lot richer.”<br><br>♥ "He read? Oh my God, guys that read were like unicorns. They only existed in fairy tales."<br><br>♥ "great googley moogley"<br><br>♥ “So you like me? You really do?" <br><br>I groaned, cheeks heating. “Shut up.”<br><br>♥ “You are one of those women just born with a nice ass. No amount of workouts can create this ass.” <br><br>“That’s correct,” I said after a few seconds. “I think it was Big Macs and tacos that created that ass.”<br><br>♥ “You know what else I see? A physical reminder of how fucking strong you are, Calla, how fucking brave you are. That’s what I see when I look at your back. A map of how brave you are, your strength and your courage.”<br><br>♥ "I’m pretty sure your Long Island iced teas could kill people, but that’s okay.” His lips curved up on one side as his gaze held mine steadily. “I love your sense of humor and the fact you never ate grits before. There’s so much I love about you that I know I’m in love with you. So, honey, you can have all my shirts you want.”<br><br>♥ "Jase turned his head to me, brows raised. “If I liked guys—you know, swung that way, I’d get naked after that.”<br><br>♥ “You remembered my list of stupid things.” I sat up fully and he followed. I leaned in, pressing my forehead against him. “That makes you amazing.”<br><br><br><br>♦ BR w/Melissa!<br><br><br><br><i>(Prior to Review)</i><br><br>Ollie and Brittany's story ...or Calla's and...<i>Brandon</i>?? <br><br>both please!!</span>

<div id="review_637061090" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/637061090" />
    <a title="Valerie" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4148118-valerie"><img alt="Valerie" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1364076470p2/4148118.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/637061090?book_show_action=true">Jun 09, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Valerie" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Valerie" href="/user/show/4148118-valerie">Valerie</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4148118-valerie?shelf=2014-reads">2014-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4148118-valerie?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4148118-valerie?shelf=jla">jla</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4148118-valerie?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4148118-valerie?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer637061090" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13300191024775058811"><br/><br/>I have LOVED this series, every book and guy in it. These books feature the "HOT GUY BRIGADE" (Calla's words not mine). Cam is the President (again according to Calla) because of his yummy looks and warm personality in Wait For Me. Jase is the lieutenant because of his "model good looks" and ability to make people feel "comfy" in Be With Me. Ollie gets a second to the lieutenant position for all his "antics", including leashing those adorable turtles, and his sexy ways! But just wait, because Ja</span>
  <span id="freeText13300191024775058811" style="display:none"><br /><br />I have LOVED this series, every book and guy in it. These books feature the "HOT GUY BRIGADE" (Calla's words not mine). Cam is the President (again according to Calla) because of his yummy looks and warm personality in Wait For Me. Jase is the lieutenant because of his "model good looks" and ability to make people feel "comfy" in Be With Me. Ollie gets a second to the lieutenant position for all his "antics", including leashing those adorable turtles, and his sexy ways! But just wait, because Jax has arrived and he has stolen the top position - at least he has for Calla and for me. Bet you'll agree.<br /><br />Why? Oh Jax, I so love you.<br /><br />A former Marine, Jax has a protective streak. And when Calla ends up in some serious trouble, he's all about keeping her safe. The boy can handle a gun and roll with the best of them. Speaking of safe, he's willing to be Call's safe place for all those things she's never tried. It takes her some time to trust him but he is so trustworthy. A nice guy with some bada$$ abilities, he's not perfect but he tries.<br /><br />Something that he is perfect with is the kissing. He loves doing it and has perfected the art. Oh and cuddling, the boy's a cuddler, a snuggler. He's not so much a morning person, that's sleepy time but once he's awake it must be lovin' time. Did I mention how deeply he cares for Calla. Yeah, he likes her...like a lot. She likes him too but is afraid.<br /><br />Calla has some things that she hasn't shared with her friends. There is more to the scar on her face than everyone knows. So getting naked with a guy is so not going to happen. But enter very patient Jax and things begin to be crossed off that never done before list, like her first kiss.<br /><br />Something that makes Jax so different is his sincere ability to help Calla feel comfortable with who she is. He loves her humor and he thinks she's cute, often. He tells her. I was very impressed with this part of him. <br /><br />Something usual book was the amount of snuggles and cuddles that went on BEFORE anything else happened. Jax has a connection with Calla that I knew meant more than we knew though I wasn't sure what it was till the end. It's sweet.<br /><br />I loved how Jax was trustworthy. Calla doubted him a few times, but I never did. That boy is real and part of that realness was communication. So many books have some silly misunderstanding that keeps the couple apart. Jax wants Calla to be on the same page with him all the time. He wants her right there with him. He wants her coming to HIM when something between them upsets her. I loved that. <br /><br />The characters from the previous books are part of this story but we meet some new characters that I love. I want to know what's up with Reese and Roxy. I love the brooding Nick. <br /><br />By far, the most amusing character was Katie. She bounced in every once in a while and certainly livened things up. I can hope that some of these characters will move on to other books in the series. Especially Reese and Roxy. WANTS!<br /><br />This is a long book, over 400 pages, but I was so into it that it never felt long. The story is full of so much more than a romance. There's a very present danger that Calla finds herself in. There's mystery as to what is really going on with her mom and the bar. There's people threatening her and a dead body showing up on her doorstep and even worry from loved ones. So much for poor Calla to have to deal with all the while falling for the sexy Jax. Loved it.<br /><br />My favorite of the series, Stay With Me brings the sexy and the emotional. It had me falling in love and worried about some very real feeling characters. It had me laughing out loud for reals. It had me wanting to trust Jax and wanting to slap Calla for doubting him. It had me questioning how things could ever work out but hoping with all my fingers and toes crossed that it would.<br /><br />Just as Jennifer got better and better with every paranormal book she has written, her NA books have done the same thing. Stay With Me rocks the sexy, humor, and drama into a satisfying read that just has you smiling as you close the book. Don't miss this one!<br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="13300191024775058811" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/33526516-ramona-popescu?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1168146613" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer1122761888171261820">Once you get a bite of the forbidden fruit, you develop this addiction that makes you read Jennifer’s series in a flash!! This happened to me and I loved every minute of every story because they are nothing alike, except the awesomeness that binds them.<br/><br/>“Stay with me” is the third installment and follows Calla, Teresa and Avery’s friend. Calla is very different from her friends and the situations she will be put in are different, making her a very fierce heroine, but also vulnerable and sweet.<br/><br/>Cal</span>
  <span id="freeText1122761888171261820" style="display:none">Once you get a bite of the forbidden fruit, you develop this addiction that makes you read Jennifer’s series in a flash!! This happened to me and I loved every minute of every story because they are nothing alike, except the awesomeness that binds them.<br><br>“Stay with me” is the third installment and follows Calla, Teresa and Avery’s friend. Calla is very different from her friends and the situations she will be put in are different, making her a very fierce heroine, but also vulnerable and sweet.<br><br>Calla always lived wearing a mask and she didn’t revel her true colors to anyone, not even to Teresa and Avery. She had an accident as a child that left her with a scar on her cheek and because of this, she is ashamed of her physical appearance. She wears make- up a lot, but she also hides her true self. She is very shy, never shared a kiss with a boy, never enjoyed herself in the true way of the word. Everything changes when she hears about her mom and she is forced to return to her home town, a place she wants to forget more than anything. Here she will meet Jax, who is running her mom’s local business, a diner. They hit it off immediately, but as I’ve mentioned before, Calla is very shy and Jax can be extremely intimidating when he want to. And guess what? He wants Calla 🙂<br><br>Jax and Calla have an amazing chemistry and development in their relationship. Calla has been through a lot in her life and I felt extremely sorry for her about what happened to her. Jax was there for her and really made a mission in life to change her perspective upon life and priorities. He shows her how to accept herself and just let go everything clouding her future, and believe me, she faced some serious traumas. He made her believe in her beauty as well, embrace her physical imperfections and live proud with them, a mark of how brave she was and the amazing development she had. Fantastic right? Calla will bloom in Jax arms, but the road is very hard and with a lot of obstacles and secrets when places never thought about before.<br><br>I have to admit that the plot was more alert and had a slightly dangerous vibe to it. There were particular moments when I was really scared and feared the worst for our characters. But after drawing the line, the story was very complex and had everything I needed to mark it with 5 stars.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1479123324i/21149668._SX540_.png" width="500" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>For more reviews please check <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://readwithloveblog.wordpress.com">https://readwithloveblog.wordpress.com</a></span>

<div id="review_1138534016" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1138534016" />
    <a title="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4197769-jacqueline-s-reads"><img alt="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1380942477p2/4197769.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1138534016?book_show_action=true">Dec 22, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" href="/user/show/4197769-jacqueline-s-reads">Jacqueline&#39;s Reads</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/19407085-stay-with-me">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1138534016" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14457978457245845387"><b>3, I don’t know where to begin stars</b><br/><br/>I usually love Jennifer’s books. I’m a major fan of this series, but something about Stay with Me just rubbed me the wrong way. It wasn’t a bad book, but maybe I just wasn’t in the right mood.<br/><br/>First off, it’s VERY VERY VERY LONG…. It took me about 6 weeks to read it. I kept on taking breaks during the boring parts.<br/><br/>Yes, it was kind of boring. There are some good moments, but there are a lot of dragging parts.<br/><br/>I also had an issue with the storyline. I couldn’t get</span>
  <span id="freeText14457978457245845387" style="display:none"><b>3, I don’t know where to begin stars</b><br><br>I usually love Jennifer’s books. I’m a major fan of this series, but something about Stay with Me just rubbed me the wrong way. It wasn’t a bad book, but maybe I just wasn’t in the right mood.<br><br>First off, it’s VERY VERY VERY LONG…. It took me about 6 weeks to read it. I kept on taking breaks during the boring parts.<br><br>Yes, it was kind of boring. There are some good moments, but there are a lot of dragging parts.<br><br>I also had an issue with the storyline. I couldn’t get into it and I couldn’t sympathize with the Heroine.<br><br> <b>Summary</b><br><br>Calla’s mom basically used her savings for drugs. So, Calla doesn’t have money for college. Calla goes back home to track down her mom and get her money back.<br><br>When she goes home, she realizes she’s mixed up with some bad people because of her mom.<br><br>Jax works at the bar Calla’s mom owns and is helping Calla track down her mom.<br><br><b>Calla</b><br><br>I didn’t like Calla. First off, if you had a drug addicted mom who is no good for you, why would you give her access to your funds? You really did forget? This is your future and you are just careless like that? Second off, your mom pretends to be you and messes up your credit. Can’t you go to the police and get that fixed and try to get a student loan? I don’t know, just shooting out ideas.<br><br>So Calla goes back to her old home and it’s really not safe. There’s druggies knocking at her door, but does she stay with Jax when he tries to help her out? No. She’s stubborn. Honestly, if some druggie showed up at my childhood home and a sexy bartender is willing to let me stay at his place, I would pick the sexy bartender, that’s just me. Pride or not.<br><br>Then, Calla has image issues. She was in an accident and it left her with a scar on her face and body. I get it. I so get it. It makes her really really really self-conscious, but she whines about it the WHOLE book (oh and the cover doesn’t even match the description). Jax keeps on telling her how beautiful she is, but she’s like whine whine, no I am not. **eye roll** please.<br><br><b>Overall</b><br><br>I liked Jax and I didn’t see why he would be interested in Calla. Sure she’s different and smart, but other than that, I don’t see the appeal.<br><br> Jax and Calla work together to track down Calla’s mom. I am indifferent with this storyline. I think it’s because I find this to be a romance novel, not some YA book where the good guys are trying to track down the villain. It just adds too much volume to the read and I seriously wanted it to end.<br><br>I still love the author and the series is still a favorite of mine, I just hope this one was just a fluke and the next one is a lot shorter.<br><br><b>Series Order<br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17314430.Wait_for_You__Wait_for_You___1_" title="Wait for You (Wait for You, #1) by J. Lynn" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1363819713s/17314430.jpg" alt="Wait for You (Wait for You, #1) by J. Lynn" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a> <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/550500887" rel="nofollow noopener">REVIEW</a> | <a href="http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B00C3342T2/ref=as_li_qf_sp_asin_tl?ie=UTF8&amp;camp=211189&amp;creative=373489&amp;creativeASIN=B00C3342T2&amp;link_code=as3&amp;tag=jacqsread-20" rel="nofollow noopener">AMAZON</a><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17860217.Trust_in_Me__Wait_for_You___1_5_" title="Trust in Me (Wait for You, #1.5) by J. Lynn" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1376561229s/17860217.jpg" alt="Trust in Me (Wait for You, #1.5) by J. Lynn" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a> <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/695577557" rel="nofollow noopener">REVIEW</a> | <a href="http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B00CKOVAV2/ref=as_li_qf_sp_asin_tl?ie=UTF8&amp;camp=211189&amp;creative=373489&amp;creativeASIN=B00CKOVAV2&amp;link_code=as3&amp;tag=jacqsread-20" rel="nofollow noopener">AMAZON</a></b><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17558817.Be_with_Me__Wait_for_You___2_" title="Be with Me (Wait for You, #2) by J.   <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1380210727s/17558817.jpg" alt="Be with Me (Wait for You, #2) by J. Lynn" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/610378245" rel="nofollow noopener">REVIEW</a> | <a href="http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B00DB3D99M/ref=as_li_tl?ie=UTF8&amp;camp=211189&amp;creative=373489&amp;creativeASIN=B00DB3D99M&amp;link_code=as3&amp;tag=jacqsread-20&amp;linkId=PGYXNVZNGKW6FF7I" rel="nofollow noopener">AMAZON</a><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/19501672.Stay_with_Me__Wait_for_You___3_" title="Stay with Me (Wait for You, #3) by J. <div id="review_1062594478" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1062594478" />
    <a title="Alyssa" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/8472395-alyssa"><img alt="Alyssa" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1500935920p2/8472395.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1062594478?book_show_action=true">Sep 23, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Alyssa" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Alyssa" href="/user/show/8472395-alyssa">Alyssa</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8472395-alyssa?shelf=2014-releases">2014-releases</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1062594478" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9469435343995396192">***<a href='http://eaterofbooks.blogspot.com/2014/09/blog-tour-review-stay-with-me-by-j-lynn.html' rel='nofollow noopener'>Review posted on The Eater of Books! blog</a>***<br/><br/>Stay With Me by J. Lynn<br/>Book Three of the Wait For You series<br/>Publisher: William Morrow<br/>Publication Date: September 23, 2014<br/>Rating: 4 stars<br/>Source: eARC from Edelweiss<br/><br/>Official Summary:<br/><br/>From the #1 New York Times bestselling author of Wait for You and Be with Me comes a daring tale that pushes boundaries . . .<br/><br/>At 21, Calla hasn't done a lot of things. She’s never been kissed, never seen the ocean, never gone to an amusement park. But growing up, she witnes</span>
  <span id="freeText9469435343995396192" style="display:none">***<a href="http://eaterofbooks.blogspot.com/2014/09/blog-tour-review-stay-with-me-by-j-lynn.html" rel="nofollow noopener">Review posted on The Eater of Books! blog</a>***<br /><br />Stay With Me by J. Lynn<br />Book Three of the Wait For You series<br />Publisher: William Morrow<br />Publication Date: September 23, 2014<br />Rating: 4 stars<br />Source: eARC from Edelweiss<br /><br />Official Summary:<br /><br />From the #1 New York Times bestselling author of Wait for You and Be with Me comes a daring tale that pushes boundaries . . .<br /><br />At 21, Calla hasn't done a lot of things. She’s never been kissed, never seen the ocean, never gone to an amusement park. But growing up, she witnessed some things no child ever should. She still carries the physical and emotional scars of living with a strung-out mother, Mona—secrets she keeps from everyone, including her close circle of college friends.<br /><br />But the safe cocoon Calla has carefully built is shattered when she discovers her mom has stolen her college money and run up a huge credit card debt in her name. Now, Calla has to go back to the small town she thought she’d left behind and clean up her mom’s mess again. Of course, when she arrives at her mother’s bar, Mona is nowhere to be found. Instead, six feet of hotness named Jackson James is pouring drinks and keeping the place humming.<br /><br />Sexy and intense, Jax is in Calla’s business from the moment they meet, giving her a job and helping her search for Mona. And the way he looks at her makes it clear he wants to get horizontal . . . and maybe something more. Before Calla can let him get close, though, she’s got to deal with the pain of the past—and some very bad guys out to mess her up if she doesn't give them her mom.<br /><br />What I Liked:<br /><br />Okay by now, you all have to know how much I have struggled with New Adult contemporary romance. Ever since the dawn of New Adult, I have basically disliked the vast majority of the NA contemporary romance novels out there, because they are all extremely formulaic, generic, carbon copies of each others... yawn. I definitely thought that was the case with JLA's Wait For You, and Trust In Me, but Be With Me was different, which I liked. I had a good feeling about this book, to be honest.<br /><br />Calla is a friend of Teresa's, and she has a completely different life compared to Teresa and Avery's lives. Calla's mother drained Calla's bank account of all the money Calla had (which she needed to ay tuition) to buy drugs and whatnot. Calla goes home for the summer to clear things up, but only to find her bank account empty, her mother gone, the house (which Calla has not been to in years) a sanctuary for holding drugs... nothing in Calla's life is safe, or good. Jax, the guy who works at her mother's bar with Calla's uncle Clyde, looks out for Calla in so many ways. But drug kingpins are no joke, and Calla's mother is in deep, which is pretty problematic for Calla.<br /><br />I love that this book isn't focused solely on the romance, or the heroine's tragic past, or whatever. It bothers me a little, how each of JLA's heroines of this series (so far) are all *severely* damaged in some way (rape, domestic abuse, first-degree burns and scar down the face), because it makes it seem like the majority of the population of college girls go through something as SERIOUSLY damaging as these three girls did... which isn't necessarily the case. Don't trivialize horrific life events. Not that I think JLA is doing that. Anyway.<br /><br /> Calla has a unique and tragic past, just like Avery and Teresa. Calla's house wasn't perfectly stable in its electric cables or something, so it basically blew up in Calla's face (literally), killing her two brothers and mangling her skin. Her father left her mother about a year later, and her mother turned to drugs. Years later, Calla's mother drained her bank account, and owes millions of dollars to the drug lord Isaiah. <br /><br />This is the central issue of the book. Calla needs to figure out how to pay for her tuition, and how to not get caught in Mona's crazy crap... although, she is already involved, just by coming home. Calla wouldn't have survived coming back if not for Uncle Clyde, Jax, Roxy, and Katie (all new characters). Uncle Clyde is the rock in Calla's life. Roxy and Katie are amazing friends, and support Calla always.<br /><br />Jax... Jax might be my favorite hero of this NA series. Jax doesn't necessarily have a troubled past himself, but he lives in this town - he knows too much about drugs and interactions and getting violent and getting information and all of that. He was never involved with drug dealers or drugs in general, but it's tough growing up in that atmosphere. He's a Marine (sexy man in a uniform), and he is quite the guy. I really like him. He's super honest, super blunt, super nice, gentle, affectionate... not entirely the macho alpha type, though he is. In a quieter sense.<br /><br />While I mentioned that the romance isn't the only thing going on, it's totally there, and it's important. Jax and Calla fall in love, but it's not easy for Calla. Being scarred... she doesn't see herself as "pretty", but Jax doesn't care about her scars. He appreciates them, and sees the beauty in them (honestly, that makes sense, especially for someone who was involved in the Marines Corp). I really like the romance, because it isn't about two people who are lost and find each other and themselves. Calla might seem a little lost, but the romance is more about two people that find each other and go from there. Instant connection, but slow growth of relationship.<br /><br />This book is seriously long, but the story is really great. JLA is a really good storyteller, I have to give her that. She's written so many books and even though a lot of her characters start to sound the same, the stories always vary. Which is fantastic! I'll definitely be reading the next book in the series, when it comes time.<br /><br />What I Did Not Like:<br /><br />I mentioned a few things above - I almost wish the heroines that JLA creates in this particular NA series weren't so far on the extremes of having tragic pasts or being damaged or whatever. Not every college girl has life-threatening or body-endangering experiences like Avery, Teresa, and Calla all have. Seriously, I promise.<br /><br />Also - JLA's heroines totally all sound the same, after a while. Katy = Avery = Teresa = Calla = Maddie = Sydney = Layla = Samantha = Serena. Not going to lie, it gets old really fast.<br /><br />Would I Recommend It:<br /><br />Sure, sure, if you like New Adult contemporary romance, if you like JLA, sure! If you're not a fan of NA contemporary romance, then ehhh, your life won't change if you read this one, your life won't change if you don't read it. If that makes sense!<br /><br />Rating:<br /><br />4 stars. This is definitely the best book of this series yet. There is so much more depth to the story, and the romance really isn't central (in my opinion). Love that direction that JLA is taking her New Adult contemporary romance novels!</span>
  <a data-text-id="9469435343995396192" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1628688249" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1628688249" />
    <a title="Lover of Romance" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3709091-lover-of-romance"><img alt="Lover of Romance" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1458253423p2/3709091.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1628688249?book_show_action=true">May 04, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lover of Romance" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lover of Romance" href="/user/show/3709091-lover-of-romance">Lover of Romance</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1628688249" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4184846468667754565">This review was originally posted on<a href='http://addictedtoromance.org/2016/05/07/book-review-stay-with-me-by-j-lynn/' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'> Addicted To Romance</a><a href='http://addictedtoromance.org/wp-content/uploads/2016/05/My-Review-Updated-2.jpg' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1462623369i/19021958._SX540_.jpg' alt='My Review Updated' width='600' height='100' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/> 
  <em>
    <strong>Summary </strong>
  </em>
 <br/>Calla has never really had the chance to live a life she has wanted to, but she has a "bucket list" of items she desperately desires to do. Calla has been working hard to forget her life previously to coming to college and the painful memories it brings. She is focusing on her nursing education and spending time with her friends. Friends that she tells no real truths about herself with. But when her past comes back</span>
  <span id="freeText4184846468667754565" style="display:none">This review was originally posted on<a href="http://addictedtoromance.org/2016/05/07/book-review-stay-with-me-by-j-lynn/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"> Addicted To Romance</a><a href="http://addictedtoromance.org/wp-content/uploads/2016/05/My-Review-Updated-2.jpg" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1462623369i/19021958._SX540_.jpg" alt="My Review Updated" width="600" height="100" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br> 
  <em>
    <strong>Summary </strong>
  </em>
 <br>Calla has never really had the chance to live a life she has wanted to, but she has a "bucket list" of items she desperately desires to do. Calla has been working hard to forget her life previously to coming to college and the painful memories it brings. She is focusing on her nursing education and spending time with her friends. Friends that she tells no real truths about herself with. But when her past comes back to bite her in the behind, she is forced to return home and face up to real facts. Her mother is on the run, messed up with some dangerous people, took everything Calla had financially, and now Calla is in debt and has little money. She ends up returning to the bar her mother, Mona owns a place she tried long and hard to forget. Then she meets the man who runs it, Jax. Jax is sex on a stick....sexy, drop dead gorgeous and built with lean muscle and with the most gorgeous lips and brows that Calla can't get enough of. He knows how desperate her situation is, and he knows her more than he lets on. But when Calla's life is threatened because of the bad people Mona is messed up with, Calla has no choice but to lean on the one man who can protect her. Will Calla find a love she never dreamed of finding and getting a happy ever after she deserves or will her past ruin any chance of a future with Jax?<br> 
  <em>
    <strong>The Hero </strong>
  </em>
 <br>Jaxon James is a man who has seen some horrors in his life. He grew up in a mining town and enlisted in the military, never wanting a part of that small town life. Jaxon discovered true horrors once he enlisted into the marines and went on tours. He saw horrific things happens and lost close friends and managed to save the life of his closest buddy Reece. But Jaxon is still haunted at times by his time in the military. Now he works a bar, has rebuilt it from the druggy's that worked there into a reputable business. But Jaxon is holding back from Calla, a woman he wants more than life itself. He knows that this is not the place for her, its not safe. He understands the dealing that Mona has had for years, but Jaxon is determined to keep the woman he loves safe at all cost. Now Jaxon was a hero you would want to marry----swoon worthy, but honorable, kind and so nice. He can be a bit alpha at times, but I felt like it was not overkill and really balanced him out. In the past he has been a bit of a man whore at times, but when you understand why, it becomes understandable in the end and I admired his strength and protective instincts and loved the way he was with Calla.<br><blockquote>
  <em>
    <strong>“I gotta tell you that I love you, Calla,” he said, and I was surprised the heart monitor didn’t catch the fact it felt like my heart had stopped for a moment. “No bullshit. I do. I love the way you think, even if it’s annoying as fuck at times and even then it’s still cute. I love that there’s a shit ton of things you’ve never gotten to experience and that you’re going to get to experience them with me. That I have that honor. I love your strength and everything you’ve survived. I love your courage and I love that you make shit drinks, but no one cares, because you’re so damn nice.</strong>
  </em>
</blockquote><br> 
  <em>
    <strong>The Heroine </strong>
  </em>
 <br>Calla is twenty one years old, and in her mind hasn't really lived much of a life. Never been kissed, never had alcohol, never eaten apple pie, or gone on a roller coaster.<br><blockquote>
  <em>
    <strong>“I've never had apple pie," I blurted out.</strong>
  </em>
  <br>
  <em>
    <strong>…</strong>
  </em>
  <br>
  <em>
    <strong>"You've never had apple pie?"</strong>
  </em>
  <br>
  <em>
    <strong>"No."</strong>
  </em>
  <br>
  <em>
    <strong>His brows rose. "Why?"</strong>
  </em>
  <br>
  <em>
    <strong>"I don't know. Just never tried it."</strong>
  </em>
  <br>
  <em>
    <strong>"That's so…so un-American," he said, and I rolled my eyes. "Are you a terrorist?” </strong>
  </em>
</blockquote><br>Her life hasn't been one where she could do those things. She has spent her whole life fixing up her mothers messes. When Calla was just a girl, her two brothers were killed in a fire and she was scarred, scars she tries desperately to cover up with the best line of makeup available. Calla's life changed after the fire. Her father deserted the family, because he couldn't deal. Her mother became a druggie and alcoholic. But when she came to college, she thought her life would change for the better and she had a plan for the future. But when that future is ruined she has no choice but to return home and try to fix her mother's problems. Calla is a heroine I instantly connected with. She has gone through a horrible childhood and teen years. I admired her inner strength and courage she has. She is very resilient, we also see some character growth in her where she truly realizes the importance of Living life instead of just existing.<br> 
  <em>
    <strong>Plot and Story Line </strong>
  </em>
 <br>Stay With Me is the third installment in the series but the first book I have picked up from this author. When I saw the audiobook avaiable through my library....I snatched it up instantly. I was hoping that it wouldn't be too much to pick up a book in the middle of the series and one thing I liked was even though I found myself intrigued by the two previous couples, I didn't feel like I had to read the previous books to read this one, it was pretty easy to catch on. Now Stay With Me was a book I was instantly drawn into. I was intrigued by the blurb, and just wanted to know more of this pair. Both Calla and Jax make such a great couple, but I just love it when an author introduces trauma into a character. It seems to add more depth to a story and boy did J.Lynn AKA Jennifer L. Armentrout really create a beautiful and heart wrenching romance story that had me listening to this audiobook as much as possible.<br><blockquote>
  <em>
    <strong>“Each time I saw you, I felt like . . . I felt like I knew you a little bit better. I never talked to you but seeing you always smiling or laughing . . . or being peaceful . . .” He shook his head, and my heart spasmed. “There’s something about that . . . it drew me in, Calla. Fuck. I fell for you before you even knew my name.” </strong>
  </em>
</blockquote><br>In fact I stayed up late yesterday finishing it up, because I couldn't take my ear buds out. The story just got better with each chapter and this pair is so perfect for each other. They both learn certain lessons that are needed for a healthy relationship. Neither of them have had a full on serious romantic relationship, so they both make mistakes but they also learn how to be better partners for each other along the way as they stumble and fall but they get right back up and keep working at it. This aspect is what I loved most, neither Jax or Calla gave up on the love they discovered for each other. They keep fighting for it even if they make stupid mistakes. But we also get a "dangerous" aspect added to the story line that really added to the story and didn't detract from it. I love a good mystery and suspense and boy did I enjoy this portion of the story so much!!! The humor was fantastic and I had so many bursts of laughter from the dry humor that was put in the story that really lightened up some more serious tones of it. This was quite a remarkable romance to read and I can't wait to pick up the rest of the series!!<br> 
  <em>
    <strong>The Cover </strong>
  </em>
 <br>WOW!! I really love this cover, because that pose....man I LOVE it!! Its so *sigh* fantastic and it makes you give a double take when you look at it. Very compelling.<br> 
  <em>
    <strong>Overall View </strong>
  </em>
 <br>Stay With Me is a compelling and heart wrenching romance that will leave you spellbound from the first pages. A love story that shows the strength of love, and showing its readers that the right love is worth fighting for.  A PROFOUND ROMANCE!!<br><br><a href="http://addictedtoromance.org/wp-content/uploads/2016/05/Series-Order-2-1.jpg" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1462623369i/19021959._SX540_.jpg" alt="Series Order (2)" width="600" height="100" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>[foogallery id="21418"]<br><br><a href="http://addictedtoromance.org/wp-content/uploads/2016/05/About-The-Author-Updated-1.jpg" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1462623369i/19021960._SX540_.jpg" alt="About The Author Updated" width="600" height="100" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="http://addictedtoromance.org/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1458993224i/18557444.jpg" alt=" photo Addicted To Romance Reviews 2_zpsplp8m0tb.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>

<div id="review_1063913979" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1063913979" />
    <a title="Chelsea ❤Peril Please❤ " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/8422853-chelsea-peril-please"><img alt="Chelsea ❤Peril Please❤ " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1570038444p2/8422853.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1063913979?book_show_action=true">Sep 25, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Chelsea ❤Peril Please❤ " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Chelsea ❤Peril Please❤ " href="/user/show/8422853-chelsea-peril-please">Chelsea ❤Peril Please❤ </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8422853-chelsea-peril-please?shelf=my-favorite-covers">my-favorite-covers</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8422853-chelsea-peril-please?shelf=unforgettable-male-leads">unforgettable-male-leads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8422853-chelsea-peril-please?shelf=buddy-read">buddy-read</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1063913979" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3445513731859429586"><b>*3.5 Stars*</b><br/><br/><b>
  <i>Lifting my gaze, I met his. "I don't want to think."<br/>Jax didn't question or comment on this. There was a flare of something hot and heady in his eyes, and then he dipped his mouth to mine, and he kissed me sweetly-the kind of kiss that went beyond the heavy and sensual ones. It meant something, and I seemed to open up to it, really feeling it, believing in it.<br/>And that was pretty damn spectacular.</i>
</b><br/><br/>Okay, so, I've gotten super picky lately...I mean <i>super</i> picky. A year ago, this would h</span>
  <span id="freeText3445513731859429586" style="display:none"><b>*3.5 Stars*</b><br><br><b>
  <i>Lifting my gaze, I met his. "I don't want to think."<br>Jax didn't question or comment on this. There was a flare of something hot and heady in his eyes, and then he dipped his mouth to mine, and he kissed me sweetly-the kind of kiss that went beyond the heavy and sensual ones. It meant something, and I seemed to open up to it, really feeling it, believing in it.<br>And that was pretty damn spectacular.</i>
</b><br><br>Okay, so, I've gotten super picky lately...I mean <i>super</i> picky. A year ago, this would have been hands down 5 stars and no other book could touch it. But I have kind of fallen out of J. Armentrout's spell, and that makes me sad...but it also helps to not be in a haze and to be able to see what works for me with my formerly favorite author and what doesn't. A lot of people will disagree with me, but, and this is a <b>large</b> but...I think Armentrout shines in the paranormal romance genre. I think she produces her best work there. And that's not to say that her NA books aren't good, they are. But, when reading her NA vs. her Paranormal YA, I just connect way more and feel more passion from her Lux and Dark Elements and Covenants series. The things that bother me with her writing tend to prickle me less when it's in a paranormal setting as opposed to her NA worlds. <br><br><b>"What does it taste like?" I resisted.<br>"Grits."<br>I lowered my fork, looking at him blandly. "Details."<br>He laughed as he cut through what looked like ten pancakes stacked. "One cannot simply describe grits. One must simply enjoy them."<br>My eyes rolled, but I scooped up a small taste, made sure I had cheese in it, and gingerly tasted them. The whole time Jax watched and waited. I swallowed, unsure of what to think. I tried a little more.<br>"So?" he asked.<br>"I don't know." I shoved a mouthful in. "I haven't decided yet. I think they taste good, but they're called grits; therefore I'm not sure I can freely admit to liking something called grits. I have to really think about this."<br>Jax laughed. "Cute."</b><br><br>I think it has to do with the subject matter. Her Wait for You books tend to lean on the heavier side with humor laced throughout, but I think the inner dialogue doesn't quite...go...whereas for her paranormal books they aren't normally quite so gravid. So when she wants to throw in a funny saying during an epic battle, you aren't quite so focused on it-you're waiting for the next blow as opposed to the next emotional twist or turn. Those happen too, in her para, but not near as heavily as these NAs.<br><br><b>"You're not going to be a message. You aren't going to be shit to any of them. You feel me? No one is touching you," he said, and he said it right in front of Nick. He touched me right in front of Nick, touched my scar. "We're going to take care of this and none of this shit is going to rub off on you. Okay?" </b><br><br>That's not to say I didn't enjoy this book, because I did. No, it wasn't my favorite work of hers, but it still had an <b>amazing male lead</b> and a fun cast surrounding her. Can we just take a minute to acknowledge that J. Armentrout creates literally the <b>best</b> male leads?? If there is one thing I can always count on, it's her ability to create guys that make my knees weak. I do have to admit he was my favorite part of this whole story. Jax was sexy, protective, swoony, sweet, determined, and passionate about his goals. &lt;&lt;&lt; Hey, I think we forget about those goal oriented fellas these days....it's still an admirable trait!!! I loved how he respected her and protected her even when she was trying to be stubborn and refused his help. I'm in love with guys that are overly protective without being annoying, so of course he was a total win for me.<br><br><b>I sucked in a sharp breath that hurt. He'd done this before, too, and it created the same maelstrom of emotion in me, but he did more this time. His lips followed that scar all the way down my cheek, right to the corner of my left lip, and then he kissed me. It was soft and sweet and it lingered. My hands went to his chest and I leaned into him.<br>When he lifted his mouth from mine and pressed his forehead against mine, tears had built in the back of my throat. "I don't care about it, Calla. I don't even think about it," he said. "I don't even see it."</b><br><br>Ack, okay, my biggest complaint-I don't like when authors build up to something epic....and then it just...<i>isn't.</i> Like, why build it up at all??? Maybe I am a tad masochistic and do tend to like the dramatic, crazy endings of dystopian or sci-fi or paranormal better, but they are fifty times more satisfying than a boring and almost unrealistic talk-it-out ending...okay....hmmm....Maybe I'm getting my reality mixed up lol. I think I've been spending too much time in my fantasy world, but, eh, I still would like <i>something</i> crazy to happen at the end if it's built up that way.<br><br><b>Jax's chuckle brushed the back of my neck as he pulled me back tighter against him so that there was no space between us at all. "You still with me?"<br>"I'm still with you."</b><br><br>So, that's my spiel. I liked it, didn't love. There was a certain point where I fell in love with it, but five minutes later I was lukewarm again. I was very up and down with my likes and loves for this'n. I feel so very fickle, but all in all I think that rating above accurately portrays my feelings throughout the entirety of the novel. A strong male lead and a fun atmosphere (the other favorite part of the story for me I didn't mention), this story had a lot going for it. For those of you who are familiar with J. Armentrout and adore her writing, you'll fall for this one as well. As for me, I do wish she could change up her sayings a bit....but, overall a really fun story that most will enjoy.<br><br><br><i>For more of my reviews, please visit:</i><br><a href="http://starcrossedbookblog.com/chelsea/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img height="200" width="320" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1491628712i/22430034._SX540_.jpg" alt="descriptive text here" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <u>
  <b></b>
</u><br><a href="http://starcrossedbookblog.com/chelsea/%20" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img height="60" width="139" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1409285880i/10960212.jpg" alt="descriptive text here" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <u>
  <b></b>

<span id="freeTextContainer5561555276409822066">I finished this series very confused. I mean I had this feeling while reading the whole book. I really don’t know why. Maybe it had to do something with the action taking place in a different city than the two other books? I have no idea... <br/>But - there’s always a but - this doesn’t mean that I didn’t like the book. Au contraire! I did like it. There was always something happening out of the blue that I didn’t expect. And of course Jax. He made it easy for me to love some parts of the book. <br/>Why d</span>
  <span id="freeText5561555276409822066" style="display:none">I finished this series very confused. I mean I had this feeling while reading the whole book. I really don’t know why. Maybe it had to do something with the action taking place in a different city than the two other books? I have no idea... <br />But - there’s always a but - this doesn’t mean that I didn’t like the book. Au contraire! I did like it. There was always something happening out of the blue that I didn’t expect. And of course Jax. He made it easy for me to love some parts of the book. <br />Why do male characters always succeed in absorbing me into a book?! They aren’t real! And still - they feel soooo real! 😏</span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('2u0WTn1QlY2Sli85Lzhvk6VkVRhRa0uin8Y2oqLsGrSLTa4WhF1Gz+S05aU7awRLnySZOH9JGK+EoTd2ODiqcg==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('26GRIEfHRyxX38MHbPEOrrgcqjcPqNTEsPHevvM1x42KASl4vsqUbiH9CZt4omV2glxmFyGKh8mrlt9qaeF3Sw==')})
  }
//]]>

<span id="freeTextContainer12814598814583205966">Hey Guys! Please note: I don't send out ARCs for review. If you're interested in reviewing a book of mine before release date, please contact the appropriate publisher. I also do NOT check my Goodreads email.<br/><br/>To email me, please use the below addy. <br/>jenniferlarmentrout@live.com<br/><br/># 1 New York Times and # 1 International Bestselling author Jennifer lives in Charles Town, West Virginia. All the rumors yo</span>
  <span id="freeText12814598814583205966" style="display:none">Hey Guys! Please note: I don't send out ARCs for review. If you're interested in reviewing a book of mine before release date, please contact the appropriate publisher. I also do NOT check my Goodreads email.<br /><br />To email me, please use the below addy. <br />jenniferlarmentrout@live.com<br /><br /># 1 New York Times and # 1 International Bestselling author Jennifer lives in Charles Town, West Virginia. All the rumors you’ve heard about her state aren’t true. When she’s not hard at work writing. she spends her time reading, watching really bad zombie movies, pretending to write, hanging out with her husband and her Jack Russell Loki. In early 2015, Jennifer was diagnosed with retinitis pigmentosa, a group of rare genetic disorders that involve a breakdown and death of cells in the retina, eventually resulting in loss of vision, among other complications. Due to this diagnosis, educating people on the varying degrees of blindness has become of passion of hers, right alongside writing, which she plans to do as long as she can. <br /><br />Her dreams of becoming an author started in algebra class, where she spent most of her time writing short stories….which explains her dismal grades in math. Jennifer writes young adult paranormal, science fiction, fantasy, and contemporary romance. She is published with Tor, HarperCollins Avon and William Morrow, Entangled Teen and Brazen, Disney/Hyperion and Harlequin Teen. Her Wicked Series has been optioned by PassionFlix. Jennifer has won numerous awards, including the 2013 Reviewers Choice Award for Wait for You, the 2015 Editor’s Pick for Fall With Me, and the 2014/2015 Moerser-Jugendbuch- Jury award for Obsidian. Her young adult romantic suspense novel DON’T LOOK BACK was a 2014 nominated Best in Young Adult Fiction by YALSA. Her adult romantic suspense novel TILL DEATH was a Amazon Editor’s Pick and iBook Book of the Month. Her young adult contemporary THE PROBLEM WITH FOREVER is a 2017 RITA Award Winner in Young Adult Fiction. She also writes Adult and New Adult contemporary and paranormal romance under the name J. Lynn. She is published by Entangled Brazen and HarperCollins.<br /><br />She is the owner of ApollyCon and The Origin Event, the successful annual events that features over hundred bestselling authors in Young Adult, New Adult, and Adult Fiction, panels, parties, and more.</span>

The same night her childhood love, Brock ‘the Beast’ Mitchell, broke her heart, her life was irrevocably altered by the hand of a stranger with a gun. It takes six years to slowly glue together the shattered pieces of her life, but Jillian is finally ready to stop existing in a past full of pain and regret. She takes a job at her father’s martial arts Academy and she’s going out on her first date since a failed relationship that was more yuck than yum. Jillian is determined to start living.\n\nShe just never expected Brock to be a part of her life again. But he’s firmly back in her life before she knows it, and not only is he older, he’s impossibly more handsome, more teasing and more everything. And when he sees Jillian, he’s no longer capable of thinking of her as the little girl who was his shadow growing up or the daughter of the man who gave him a second chance at life. He sees the woman who’d always been there for him, the one person who believed in him no matter what.\n\nBrock knows she’s the one he should’ve made his, and what begins as a tentative friendship quickly turns to red-hot chemistry that sparks a flame that burns brighter than lust. Falling for Brock again risks more than her heart, because when the past sorrow-filled and guilt-ridden past resurfaces, and a web of lies threatens to rip them apart, the fallout could lay waste to
